    PROCEDURE InsertExtendedProperty@1100525000(TabID@1100525000 : Integer;TypeTxt@1100525001 : Text[50];FormID@1100525002 : Integer;GranTxt@1100525003 : Text[50];Dim1Field@1100525007 : Integer;Dim1FilterField@1100525008 : Integer;GranNameTxt@1100525004 : Text[50]);
    VAR
      lvTablePropInternalRec@1100525006 : Record 11020573;
      AllObjWithCaption@1100525005 : Record 2000000058;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT AllObjWithCaption.GET(AllObjWithCaption."Object Type"::Table,TabID) THEN
        EXIT;

      lvTablePropInternalRec."Table ID" := TabID;
      EVALUATE(lvTablePropInternalRec."Type of Table",TypeTxt);
      lvTablePropInternalRec."Page ID" := FormID;
      lvTablePropInternalRec.Granule := GranTxt;
      lvTablePropInternalRec."Granule Name" := GranNameTxt;
      lvTablePropInternalRec."DPA Field No." := Dim1Field;
      lvTablePropInternalRec."DPA Filter Field No." := Dim1FilterField;
      lvTablePropInternalRec.INSERT;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {

      Manual changes will be overruled next release process.
